
======================================================================

Ballog'Nath, the Hellfire
is a unique
Boss
creature that can be found either in the
Buried Crypt
or the Rover Camp in the
Rotting Croplands
,  depending on the player's actions when they are talking to
Kalista
. Killing Ballog'Nath is necessary to complete the
Trapped and Alone
quest.
Family:
Chthonic
Genus:
Void Fiend
Abilities:
Warp Breath
Warp Stomp
Enrage
Void Fire
Ring of Flame
Mark of Pain
Resistances
Level 4
Hero/Boss Resistances
Chaos Resistance 25%
Fire Resistance 75%
Notable Drops
Masteries

======================================================================
PAGE: Balok'Anatu, Bloodfiend
CATEGORIES: Boss Creatures, Chthonics
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Balok'Anatu,_Bloodfiend
======================================================================

Balok'Anatu, Bloodfiend
is a unique
Boss
creature that can be found in the
Bastion of Chaos
.
He is guarding the way to the second level:
Discord
.
Family:
Chthonic
Genus:
Void Leech
Abilities
Charge
Life Drain
Challenging Roar
Double Swipe
Devouring Nova
Chaos Wave
Resistances
Level 4
Hero/Boss Resistances
Physical: 15%
Pierce: 15%
Chaos: 25%
Vitality: 100%
Stun: 50%
Notable Drops
Supreme Spoils
Blood of Ch'thon
Masteries

======================================================================
PAGE: Bane'Galgalor, Guardian of the Gate
CATEGORIES: Boss Creatures, Chthonics
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Bane'Galgalor,_Guardian_of_the_Gate
======================================================================

Bane'Galgalor, Guardian of the Gate
is a unique
Boss
creature that can be found in the
Tomb of the Watchers
.
He is guarding the path to the
Seal of the Loghorrean
.
Family:
Chthonic
Genus:
Void Leech
Abilities
Poison Strike
Poison Cloud
Vile Aura
Vile Spit
Resistances
Level 4
Hero/Boss Resistances
Physical: 15%
Fire: 50%
Vitality: 100%
Poison: 100%
Freeze: 500%
Knockdown: 500%
Petrify: 500%
Sleep: 500%
Stun: 500%
Trap: 500%

Grand Spoils

PAGE: Bane'Gargoth

Bane'Gargoth
is a unique
Boss
creature that can be found in the
Obsidian Throne
. He is the target of
Braving the Void
quest.
Family:
Chthonic
Genus:
Obsidian Ravager
Abilities
Impale
Flame Wave
Flame Core
Fireball Nova Barrage
Resistances
Level 4
Hero/Boss Resistances
Physical: 10%
Pierce: 25%
Fire: 30%
Chaos: 25%
Vitality: 50%
Petrify: 500%
Sleep: 500%
Stun: 500%
Knockdown: 500%

Supreme Spoils

======================================================================
PAGE: Benn'Jhar, the Colossal
CATEGORIES: Chthonics, Nemesis
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Benn'Jhar,_the_Colossal
======================================================================

Benn'Jahr, the Colossal
is a
Nemesis Spawn
of the
Chthonians
's faction.
He is an Ultra Boss of Grim Dawn so the player must be prepared for that encounter.
Family:
Chthonians
Genus:
Obsidian Ravager
Spawn Points
The Blood Grove
(Elite and Ultimate)
Village of Darkvale
(Elite and Ultimate)
Darkvale Gate
(Elite and Ultimate)
Sorrow's Bastion
Ashen Waste
Tomb of the Watchers
Depraved Sanctuary
The Forsaken Wastes
Obsidian Throne
Bastion of Chaos
Discord
Anarchy
Entropy

Cinder Wastes
Mourndale

Chaos Stomp
Impale
Obsidian Prison
Summon Cluster
Enrage
Warp Breath
Resistances
Level 5 Hero/Boss Resistances
50% Chaos Resistance
500% Reduced Knockdown Duration
20% Physical Resistance
20% Pierce Resistance
50% Poison & Acid Resistance
Notable Drops
Benn'Jahr's Pauldrons
Benn'Jahr's Shoulderguards

======================================================================
PAGE: Bloodlord Thalonis
CATEGORIES: Bloodsworn, Boss Creatures
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Bloodlord_Thalonis
======================================================================

Bloodlord Thalonis
is a unique
Boss
creature that can be found in the
Seal of the Loghorrean
. He must be killed in order to gain access to the
Edge of Madness
.
Family:
Human
Genus:
Bloodsworn
Abilities
Chaos Bolt
Curse
Nova Life Drain
Chaos Barrage
Chaos Bolt
Chaos Vortex
Summon Chthonian Harbinger
Resistances
Level 4
Hero/Boss Resistances
25% Chaos Resistance
25% Vitality Resistance
500% Reduced Freeze Duration
500% Reduced Knockdown Duration
Notable Drops
Grand Spoils
Bloodlord's Blade
Bloodsworn Sigil
Chthonic Seal of Binding
The Final Seal (note)
Masteries

======================================================================
PAGE: Bloodsworn
CATEGORIES: Chthonics
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Bloodsworn
======================================================================

For the enemy faction, see
Chthonians
.
Bloodsworn are a class of enemy
creature
. They are the
human
members of the Cult of Ch'thon, and aligned with the
Chthonians
Faction.
Quotes
"The Ch'thonic cults have been around since before the
first traveler
took to the roads. Under the Empire, they were outlawed and driven underground. Where cults were uncovered by inquisitors, the Emperor's
nightblades
would be sent to hunt down and execute the practitioners. Even so, they could not be eradicated and now they grow ever more powerful as people flock to them seeking purpose or salvation. More troubling though, I've heard tale that the cults have had success of late in calling forth the monstrous servants of their god to walk this world." -
Kuldo
"Have you run into the Bloodsworn yet? The fanatical cult devoted to the supposed elder god
Ch'thon
? The cult has existed forever; some say since before recorded history. I always thought the myth of an elder god betrayed and gruesomely dismembered was too fantastical to be anything but the stuff of theatre but since the Grim Dawn, it seems the cult has newfound power and desperate men flock to swell their ranks." -
Ulgrim
"The Cult of Ch'thon? Not a bunch of people you want to cross. Obsessed with the blood of some fallen god, or maybe it's just blood in general. Wasn't 'til I attended one of their underground meetings that I realized I was mixing with the wrong crowd; and believe me, I've been affiliated with some pretty twisted individuals before. Ran out of there before they were done with the first 'initiate'. You don't want to know what that entails." -
Direni
"Though Chthonian worship was not a new prospect on Cairn, desperate humans made willing allies for the powers of Ch'thon and so an old enemy has returned to haunt us and may well spell doom for us all.Even now as we slaughter one another, the void feeds upon the spilled blood and grows to envelop all of creation." -
Anasteria
Bloodsworn Variants

Bloodsworn Adulant
Race
Bloodsworn
Type
Common
Faction
Chthonians
Bloodsworn Adulants
are a human enemy aligned with
Chthonic
creatures.
Abilities
Bloodsworn Adulants can spawn with one of 5 different skills:
Melee Attack - deals Physical damage
Fire Orb
Chaos Orb
Poison Orb
Vitality Orb
Resistances
None.
Notable Drops
None.

Bloodsworn Doomsayer
Race
Bloodsworn
Type
Champion
Faction
Chthonians
Bloodsworn Doomsayers
are a human enemy aligned with
Chthonic
creatures.
Abilities
Default Attack
Physical Damage
Chaos Orb
1 Projectile
Chaos Damage
Doom Bolt
1.5 Meter Radius
Chaos Damage
Vitality damage
Debilitate (curse)
12 Meter Radius
8 Second Duration
1-5% Reduction to Current Life
-70% Health Regeneration
-10% Offensive Ability
-10% Defensive Ability
Resistances
None.
Notable Drops
Bloodsworn Scepter
Bloodsworn Codex
Chthonic Seal of Binding

Bloodsworn Priest
Race
Bloodsworn
Type
Champion
Faction
Chthonians
Bloodsworn Priests
are a human enemy aligned with
Chthonic
creatures.
Abilities
Chaos Orb
1 Projectile
Chaos Damage
Chthonic Sigil
2.5 Meter radius
5 second Duration
Chaos Damage
5% Reduction to Current Life
Summon
Voidfiend
3 Summon Limit
12 Second Cooldown
Summon
Voidfiend Hellion
1 Summon Limit
12 Second Cooldown
Resistances
None.

Bloodsworn Zealot
Race
Bloodsworn
Type
Champion
Faction
Chthonians
Bloodsworn Zealots
are a human enemy aligned with
Chthonic
creatures.

Default Attack
Physical Damage
Blood Lust (buff)
8 Meter Radius
5 Second Cooldown
(+8% to +15%) Physical Damage
(+8% to +20%) Total Speed
Summon
Voidfiend
3 Summon Limit
12 Second Cooldown
Resistances
None.

race.

Chthonian Devourer
Race
Chthonic
Type
Champion
Faction
Chthonians
The Ch'thonian Devourer is an abomination aptly named for its insatiable propensity to consume anything and everything it comes across. While physically weak, Devourers rely on numbers and devilishly quick movements to take down their prey.
Chthonian Devourers
are a type of
Chthonic
creature.
Abilities
Passive
Physical Damage
Poison Damage
Megachomp
Melee
Physical Damage
Chaos Damage
Life Leech
Resistances
Fire: 25%
Chaos: 25%
Vitality: 50%

Chthonian Servitor
Race
Chthonic
Type
Champion
Faction
Chthonians
Chthonian Servitors
are a type of
Chthonic
creature found in Void areas of
Act 5
and
Act 6
.
Abilities
Skill Name
Skill Type
Damage Type
Passive
Physical Damage
Vitality Damage
15% Chance of Bleeding Damage over 3 Seconds
15% Chance of +35% Vitality Damage
50% Bleeding Resistance
(8 to 14)% Chance to Deflect Projectiles
Blood Spit
Projectile
1 Projectile
1.5 Meter Radius
Physical Damage
Vitality Damage
Bleeding Damage over 2 Seconds
9-14% Reduction to Current Life
200 Life Leech
Triple Spit
Projectile
1 Projectile
5 Second Cooldown
1.5 Meter Radius
Physical Damage
Vitality Damage
Bleeding Damage over 2 Seconds
9-12% Reduction to Current Life
250 Life Leech
-10/20/20 to Total Resistances for 2 Seconds

======================================================================
PAGE: Karroz, Sigil of Ch'thon

URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Karroz,_Sigil_of_Ch'thon
======================================================================

Karroz, Sigil of Ch'thon
is a unique
Boss
creature that can be found at the end of the 2nd level of
Darkvale Gate
. Killing him is necessary to complete the
Reaping What You Sow
quest as he drops the
Karroz's Tome
quest item.
The fight against Karroz is divided in two stages:
You fight
Karroz
himself.
On death, his body is used as a portal by a Chthonian entity:
Thall'Nosh the Unraveller
.
Family:
Human
Genus:
Bloodsworn

======================================================================
PAGE: Lagoth'Ak, Harbinger of Blood
CATEGORIES: Boss Creatures, Chthonics
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Lagoth'Ak,_Harbinger_of_Blood
======================================================================

Lagoth'Ak, Harbinger of Blood
is a unique
Boss
creature located in the third level of the
Bastion of Chaos
:
Anarchy
.
He is inside a
Death Room
, so the player must kill him in order to exit the area.
Family:
Chthonic
Genus:
Chthonian Harbinger
Abilities
Summon Void Leech
Summon Void Souldrinker
Mirage
Crimson Spout
Blood Orb Fan
Blood Orb Nova
Resistances
Level 4
Hero/Boss Resistances
Physical: 30%
Pierce: 25%
Fire: 15%
Cold: 15%
Lightning: 15%
Chaos: 100%
Knockdown: 500%
Petrify: 500%
Sleep:500%
Notable Drops
Magnificent Spoils
Blood of Ch'thon
Masteries

======================================================================
PAGE: Loghorrean, the Voice of Ch'thon
CATEGORIES: Boss Creatures, Chthonics
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Loghorrean,_the_Voice_of_Ch'thon
======================================================================

The
Loghorrean, the Voice of Ch'thon
is a unique
Boss
creature located in the
Edge of Madness
.
He is the final boss for
Act 4
and must be killed to access the next difficulty and complete
The Bane of Cairn
quest.
The fight is divided into 3 phases:
with
Ulgrim
fighting at the player's side.
when Loghorrean is at 65% health, Ulgrim is consumed by the void and two
Loghorrean's Vanguard
(Hero monsters) are summoned.
at 50% Health Loghorrean gains a 10% cast and attack speed increase and starts casting
Summon Void
.
Family:
Chthonic
Genus:
Voice of Ch'Thon
Quotes
"You say this thing has been summoned before?" - Player
"Yes, many centuries ago, at the Battle of Ikon. Nobody knows for sure whether it was the Carineans performing a last desperate maneuver, or perhaps the Loghorrean was drawn to all the spilled blood, but the results were catastrophic." -
Ulgrim

Lunal'Valgoth, Steward of Darkness
is a
Chthonic
Insectoid
Boss located in the
Fringes of Sanity

Bounty: Steward of Darkness
.

======================================================================
PAGE: Obsidian Defiler
CATEGORIES: Chthonics
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Obsidian_Defiler
======================================================================

The void houses some of the most terrifying creations humans have ever had the misfortune of encountering. Among them is the gargantuan Obsidian Defiler. A Ch’thonic creature formed from the very material which makes up much of the Ch’thonian void, the Defiler is incredibly durable and brutally powerful. Its four arms will shred flesh like paper, but its true power lies within its chaotic core. Should you find yourself within reach of a Defiler, it is advisable to run.
Obsidian Defilers
are a
creature
type belonging to the
Chthonic
race.
Obsidian Defiler Variants
Obsidian Shaleborn
Obsidian Defiler
Obsidian Ravager

======================================================================
PAGE: Sharanatu, Harbinger of the Void
CATEGORIES: Boss Creatures, Chthonics
URL: https://grimdawn.fandom.com/wiki/Sharanatu,_Harbinger_of_the_Void
======================================================================

Sharanatu, Harbinger of the Void
is a unique
Boss
creature located in the secret area of the
Tomb of Korvaak
. The area is only accessible if the player has sided with
Kymon's Chosen
.
Sharanatu drops the
Eye of Korvaak
quest item required for
Kymon's Secret
.
Family:
Chthonic
Genus:
Chthonian Harbinger
Abilities
Chaos Aura
Chaos Blast
Chaos Vortex
Summon
Chthonian Devourer
Chaos Barrage
Pox
Resistances
Level 4
Hero/Boss Resistances
Physical: 25%
Pierce: 25%
Vitality: 25%
Chaos: 50%
Knockdown: 500%
Notable Drops
Grand Spoils
Eye of Korvaak
(Quest)
Blood of Ch'thon

Race
Chthonic
Type
Common
Faction
Chthonians
Void Parasites
are a type of
Chthonic
creature.

25%
Vitality:
100%

50%

Voidfiend Hellion
Race
Chthonic
Type
Champion
Faction
Chthonians
Voidfiend Hellions
are a type of
Chthonic
creature.
Abilities
Basic Attack
Physical Damage
Chaos Damage
Mark of Pain (debuff)
6 meter radius
5 Second Duration
(-15 to -33%) Total Damage
-20% Attack Speed
-10% Cast Speed
-10% Movement Speed
-500% Life Regeneration
Warp Breath
16 Meter Wave Distance
50% Chance to Fumble for 5 Seconds
Vitality Damage
Chaos Damage
Warp Stomp
3.5 Meter radius
Physical Damage
Chaos Damage
5-9% Reduction to Current Life
Stun for 0.5 - 1 seconds
Resistances
Physical: 10%
Fire: 20%
Chaos: 50%

Masteries

Voidfiend Incinerator
Race
Chthonic
Type
Champion
Faction
Chthonians
Voidfiend Incinerators
are a type of
Chthonic
creature.
Abilities
Basic Attack
Physical Damage
8% Chance of additional Chaos Damage
Mark of Pain (debuff)
6 meter radius
5 Second Duration
(-15 to -33%) Total Damage
-20% Attack Speed
-10% Cast Speed
-10% Movement Speed
-500% Life Regeneration
Chaos Blast
1 Projectile
2.5 Meter Radius
3 Second Duration
Fire damage
Chaos Damage
Resistances
Physical: 10%
Fire: 20%
Chaos: 50%

Voidlurker
Race
Chthonic
Type
Common
Faction
Chthonians
Voidlurkers
are a type of
Chthonian Fiend
.
Abilities
Basic Attack
Physical Damage
8% Chance of additional Chaos Damage
Caustic Eruption
4.8 Meter Radius
Physical Damage
Acid Damage
Poison Damage over 3 Seconds
5-9% Reduction to Current Life
Stun target for 1 Second
Resistances
Physical: 10%
Fire: 20%
Chaos: 50%

Voidlurker Blightbearer
Race
Chthonic
Type
Champion
Faction
Chthonians
Voidlurker Blightbearers
are a type of
Chthonian Fiend
.
Abilities
Basic Attack
Physical Damage
8% Chance of bonus Chaos Damage
Acid Breath
3 Second Cooldown
3.5 Meter Wave Distance
Acid Damage
Poison Damage over 5 Seconds
12/24/24% Reduced target's Resistances for 2 Seconds
Caustic Eruption
4.8 Meter Radius
Physical Damage
Acid Damage
Poison Damage over 3 Seconds
5-9% Reduction to Current Life
Stun target for 1 Second
Poison Orb
1 Projectile
2.5 Meter Radius
Acid Damage
Chaos Damage
Poison Damage over 10 Seconds
Resistances
Physical: 10%
Fire: 20%
Chaos: 50%

Voidlurker Pestilence
Race
Chthonic
Type
Champion
Faction
Chthonians
Voidlurker Pestilences
are a type of
Chthonian Fiend
.
Abilities
Basic Attack
Physical Damage
8% Chance of additional Chaos Damage
Acid Breath
3 Second Cooldown
3.5 Meter Wave Distance
Acid Damage
Poison Damage over 5 Seconds
12/24/24% Reduced target's Resistances for 2 Seconds
Caustic Eruption
4.8 Meter Radius
Physical Damage
Acid Damage
Poison Damage over 3 Seconds
5-9% Reduction to Current Life
Stun target for 1 Second
Caustic Presence
12 Second Cooldown
6 Second Buff Duration
3.5 Meter Radius
Acid Damage
15/25/25% Total Damage Reduction for 2 Seconds
+25% Total Speed
Mark of Pain (debuff)
6 meter radius
5 Second Duration
(-15 to -33%) Total Damage
-20% Attack Speed
-10% Cast Speed
-10% Movement Speed
-500% Life Regeneration
Resistances
Physical: 10%
Fire: 20%
Chaos: 50%
